SOV_Great_Game_SSR_decisions = {
  RUS_great_game_nippon_soviet_socialist_republic = {
    icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
    allowed = {
        tag = RUS
    }
    visible = {

    }
    available = {
      AND = {
        AND = {
          if = {
            limit = {
              country_exists = JAP
            }
            JAP = { 
              is_subject_of = RUS
            }
          }
          JAP = {  
            645 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            648 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            555 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            524 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            525 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            526 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            527 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            528 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            529 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            530 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            531 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            532 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            533 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            534 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            535 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            536 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            537 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
            282 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
          }
        }
        NOT = {
          JAP = { 
              has_country_flag = rus_formable 
          }
        }
      }                
    }

    cost = 30

    remove_effect = {
      hidden_effect = { 
        release = JAP
        add_political_power = 75
        JAP = { 
          set_country_flag = rus_formable
          set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_SOV_OCC
          set_politics = {
            ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
            elections_allowed = no
          }
          RUS = { 
            set_autonomy = {
              target = JAP
              autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
            }
          }
          load_focus_tree = generic_focus
        }
        JAP = { 
          every_core_state = {
            remove_core_of = JAP
          }
          645 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          648 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          555 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          524 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          525 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          526 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          527 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          528 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          529 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          530 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          531 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          532 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          533 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          534 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          535 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          536 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          537 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          282 = { add_core_of = JAP }
          JAP = { 
            every_core_state = {
              limit = {
                AND = {
                  NOT = { 
                    is_core_of = RUS
                  }
                  OR = {
                    is_owned_by = RUS
                    OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
                  }
                }
              }
              transfer_state_to = JAP
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

    days_remove = 0
    fire_only_once = yes

    ai_will_do = {
        factor = 60
    }
  }

        }
      }                
    }

    cost = 30

    remove_effect = {
      hidden_effect = { 
        release = UGA
        add_political_power = 75
        UGA = { 
          set_country_flag = rus_formable 
          # set_cosmetic_tag =  UGA_RUS_OCC 
          set_cosmetic_tag =  UGA_SOV_OCC

          }

          }
          load_focus_tree = generic_focus
        }
        UGA = { 
          every_core_state = {

          548 = { add_core_of = UGA }
          UGA = { 
            every_core_state = {
              limit = {
                AND = {
                  NOT = {

                  }
                  OR = {
                    is_owned_by = RUS
                    OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
                  }
                }
              }
              transfer_state_to = UGA
            }
          }
        }
